\frac{1+{{P_{r}}}_{t}\, {{G_{r}}}_{t}+{{Tr_r}}_{t}+{{B^G_{r}}}_{t}}{1+{{C_r}}_{t}\, {{\tau^{C}_{r}}}_{t}\, {{P_{r}}}_{t}+{{\tau^{H}_{r}}}_{t}\, {{I^H_r}}_{t}\, {{P^H_r}}_{t}+{{P^E_r}}_{t}\, {{E_r}}_{t}+{{r_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{P_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{K_{s,r}}}_{t-1}\, \left({{\tau^{K,H}_{r}}}_{t}+{{\tau^{K,F}_{s,r}}}_{t}\right)+{{LF_r}}_{t}\, {{N_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{W_{s,r}}}_{t}\, \left({{\tau^{N,H}_{r}}}_{t}+{{\tau^{N,F}_{s,r}}}_{t}\right)+{{r_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{P_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{K_{s,r}}}_{t-1}\, \left({{\tau^{K,H}_{r}}}_{t}+{{\tau^{K,F}_{s,r}}}_{t}\right)+{{LF_r}}_{t}\, {{N_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{W_{s,r}}}_{t}\, \left({{\tau^{N,H}_{r}}}_{t}+{{\tau^{N,F}_{s,r}}}_{t}\right)+{{r_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{P_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{K_{s,r}}}_{t-1}\, \left({{\tau^{K,H}_{r}}}_{t}+{{\tau^{K,F}_{s,r}}}_{t}\right)+{{LF_r}}_{t}\, {{N_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{W_{s,r}}}_{t}\, \left({{\tau^{N,H}_{r}}}_{t}+{{\tau^{N,F}_{s,r}}}_{t}\right)+{{r_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{P_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{K_{s,r}}}_{t-1}\, \left({{\tau^{K,H}_{r}}}_{t}+{{\tau^{K,F}_{s,r}}}_{t}\right)+{{LF_r}}_{t}\, {{N_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{W_{s,r}}}_{t}\, \left({{\tau^{N,H}_{r}}}_{t}+{{\tau^{N,F}_{s,r}}}_{t}\right)+{{r_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{P_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{K_{s,r}}}_{t-1}\, \left({{\tau^{K,H}_{r}}}_{t}+{{\tau^{K,F}_{s,r}}}_{t}\right)+{{LF_r}}_{t}\, {{N_{s,r}}}_{t}\, {{W_{s,r}}}_{t}\, \left({{\tau^{N,H}_{r}}}_{t}+{{\tau^{N,F}_{s,r}}}_{t}\right)+{{s_r}}_{t-1}\, \left(1+{{r^{f}}}_{t}\right)\, {{B^G_{r}}}_{t-1}}=1
\end{dmath}
% Equation 69

\frac{1+\frac{{{P^{A}_{k,r}}}_{t}}{{{P^D_{r}}}_{t}}}{1+{{\omega^{Q^A}_{k}}}^{\frac{1}{{{\eta^{Q}}}}}\, \left(\frac{{{Q^{A,F}_{k,r}}}_{t}}{{{Q^{U}_{r}}}_{t}}\right)^{\frac{\left(-1\right)}{{{\eta^{Q}}}}}}=1
\end{dmath}

\end{dmath}
% Equation 144

\begin{dmath}

\end{dmath}
